FROM (
    SELECT p.id, p.avg_rating, p.cancellation_policy, p.city, p.country, p.created_at, p.current_bookings, p.description, p.destination, p.duration_days, p.duration_nights, p.is_featured, p.max_capacity, p.min_age, p.packager_id, p.status, p.title, p.total_reviews, p.package_type, p.updated_at, (
        SELECT min(p1.base_price)
        FROM package_seasonal_pricing AS p1
        WHERE p.id = p1.package_id AND p1.is_active) AS c
    FROM packages AS p
    WHERE p.status = 'published'::package_status AND EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM package_seasonal_pricing AS p0
        WHERE p.id = p0.package_id AND p0.is_active AND p0.end_date >= @__today_0)
    ORDER BY (
        SELECT min(p1.base_price)
        FROM package_seasonal_pricing AS p1
        WHERE p.id = p1.package_id AND p1.is_active)

) AS t

    SELECT p.id, p.avg_rating, p.cancellation_policy, p.city, p.country, p.created_at, p.current_bookings, p.description, p.destination, p.duration_days, p.duration_nights, p.is_featured, p.max_capacity, p.min_age, p.packager_id, p.status, p.title, p.total_reviews, p.package_type, p.updated_at, (

FROM (
    SELECT p.id, p.avg_rating, p.cancellation_policy, p.city, p.country, p.created_at, p.current_bookings, p.description, p.destination, p.duration_days, p.duration_nights, p.is_featured, p.max_capacity, p.min_age, p.packager_id, p.status, p.title, p.total_reviews, p.package_type, p.updated_at, (
        SELECT min(p2.base_price)
        FROM package_seasonal_pricing AS p2
        WHERE p.id = p2.package_id AND p2.is_active) AS c
    FROM packages AS p
    WHERE p.status = 'published'::package_status AND EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM package_seasonal_pricing AS p0
        WHERE p.id = p0.package_id AND p0.is_active AND p0.end_date >= @__today_0) AND (lower(p.title) LIKE @__lowerTerm_1_contains OR lower(p.destination) LIKE @__lowerTerm_1_contains_1 OR lower(p.country) LIKE @__lowerTerm_1_contains_2 OR (p.city IS NOT NULL AND lower(p.city) LIKE @__lowerTerm_1_contains_2)) AND EXISTS (

        WHERE p.id = p1.package_id AND p1.is_active AND p1.available_slots > 0 AND p1.start_date <= @__request_TravelStartDate_Value_2)
    ORDER BY (
        SELECT min(p2.base_price)
        FROM package_seasonal_pricing AS p2
        WHERE p.id = p2.package_id AND p2.is_active) DESC
    LIMIT @__p_4 OFFSET @__p_3
) AS t
INNER JOIN packagers AS p3 ON t.packager_id = p3.id
LEFT JOIN package_media AS p4 ON t.id = p4.package_id
LEFT JOIN package_seasonal_pricing AS p5 ON t.id = p5.package_id
ORDER BY t.c DESC, t.id, p3.id, p4.id

SELECT t.id, t.avg_rating, t.cancellation_policy, t.city, t.country, t.created_at, t.current_bookings, t.description, t.destination, t.duration_days, t.duration_nights, t.is_featured, t.max_capacity, t.min_age, t.packager_id, t.status, t.title, t.total_reviews, t.package_type, t.updated_at, p1.id, p2.id, p2.caption, p2.category, p2.display_order, p2.file_name, p2.file_path, p2.file_size_bytes, p2.is_primary, p2.mime_type, p2.package_id, p2.uploaded_at, p3.id, p3.available_slots, p3.base_price, p3.child_price, p3.discount_percent, p3.end_date, p3.is_active, p3.package_id, p3.season_name, p3.start_date, p1.approved_at, p1.approved_by, p1.avg_rating, p1.business_license_no, p1.company_name, p1.contact_email, p1.contact_phone, p1.created_at, p1.deactivated_at, p1.deactivation_reason, p1.description, p1.total_reviews, p1.updated_at, p1.user_id, p1.website_url
FROM (
    SELECT p.id, p.avg_rating, p.cancellation_policy, p.city, p.country, p.created_at, p.current_bookings, p.description, p.destination, p.duration_days, p.duration_nights, p.is_featured, p.max_capacity, p.min_age, p.packager_id, p.status, p.title, p.total_reviews, p.package_type, p.updated_at
    FROM packages AS p
    WHERE p.status = 'published'::package_status AND EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM package_seasonal_pricing AS p0
        WHERE p.id = p0.package_id AND p0.is_active AND p0.end_date >= @__today_0)
    ORDER BY p.created_at DESC
    LIMIT @__p_2 OFFSET @__p_1
) AS t
INNER JOIN packagers AS p1 ON t.packager_id = p1.id
LEFT JOIN package_media AS p2 ON t.id = p2.package_id
LEFT JOIN package_seasonal_pricing AS p3 ON t.id = p3.package_id
ORDER BY t.created_at DESC, t.id, p1.id, p2.id

SELECT t.id, t.avg_rating, t.cancellation_policy, t.city, t.country, t.created_at, t.current_bookings, t.description, t.destination, t.duration_days, t.duration_nights, t.is_featured, t.max_capacity, t.min_age, t.packager_id, t.status, t.title, t.total_reviews, t.package_type, t.updated_at, p1.id, p2.id, p2.caption, p2.category, p2.display_order, p2.file_name, p2.file_path, p2.file_size_bytes, p2.is_primary, p2.mime_type, p2.package_id, p2.uploaded_at, p3.id, p3.available_slots, p3.base_price, p3.child_price, p3.discount_percent, p3.end_date, p3.is_active, p3.package_id, p3.season_name, p3.start_date, p1.approved_at, p1.approved_by, p1.avg_rating, p1.business_license_no, p1.company_name, p1.contact_email, p1.contact_phone, p1.created_at, p1.deactivated_at, p1.deactivation_reason, p1.description, p1.total_reviews, p1.updated_at, p1.user_id, p1.website_url
FROM (
    SELECT p.id, p.avg_rating, p.cancellation_policy, p.city, p.country, p.created_at, p.current_bookings, p.description, p.destination, p.duration_days, p.duration_nights, p.is_featured, p.max_capacity, p.min_age, p.packager_id, p.status, p.title, p.total_reviews, p.package_type, p.updated_at
    FROM packages AS p
    WHERE p.status = 'published'::package_status AND EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM package_seasonal_pricing AS p0
        WHERE p.id = p0.package_id AND p0.is_active AND p0.end_date >= @__today_0)
    ORDER BY p.created_at DESC
    LIMIT @__p_2 OFFSET @__p_1
) AS t
INNER JOIN packagers AS p1 ON t.packager_id = p1.id
LEFT JOIN package_media AS p2 ON t.id = p2.package_id
LEFT JOIN package_seasonal_pricing AS p3 ON t.id = p3.package_id
ORDER BY t.created_at DESC, t.id, p1.id, p2.id

FROM (
    SELECT p.id, p.avg_rating, p.cancellation_policy, p.city, p.country, p.created_at, p.current_bookings, p.description, p.destination, p.duration_days, p.duration_nights, p.is_featured, p.max_capacity, p.min_age, p.packager_id, p.status, p.title, p.total_reviews, p.package_type, p.updated_at
    FROM packages AS p
    WHERE p.status = 'published'::package_status AND EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM package_seasonal_pricing AS p0
        WHERE p.id = p0.package_id AND p0.is_active AND p0.end_date >= @__today_0) AND p.package_type = @__parsedType_1
    ORDER BY p.created_at DESC
    LIMIT @__p_3 OFFSET @__p_2
) AS t
INNER JOIN packagers AS p1 ON t.packager_id = p1.id
LEFT JOIN package_media AS p2 ON t.id = p2.package_id

ORDER BY t.created_at DESC, t.id, p1.id, p2.id

FROM (
    SELECT p.id, p.avg_rating, p.cancellation_policy, p.city, p.country, p.created_at, p.current_bookings, p.description, p.destination, p.duration_days, p.duration_nights, p.is_featured, p.max_capacity, p.min_age, p.packager_id, p.status, p.title, p.total_reviews, p.package_type, p.updated_at

        SELECT 1

SELECT t.id, t.avg_rating, t.cancellation_policy, t.city, t.country, t.created_at, t.current_bookings, t.description, t.destination, t.duration_days, t.duration_nights, t.is_featured, t.max_capacity, t.min_age, t.packager_id, t.status, t.title, t.total_reviews, t.package_type, t.updated_at, p1.id, p2.id, p2.caption, p2.category, p2.display_order, p2.file_name, p2.file_path, p2.file_size_bytes, p2.is_primary, p2.mime_type, p2.package_id, p2.uploaded_at, p3.id, p3.available_slots, p3.base_price, p3.child_price, p3.discount_percent, p3.end_date, p3.is_active, p3.package_id, p3.season_name, p3.start_date, p1.approved_at, p1.approved_by, p1.avg_rating, p1.business_license_no, p1.company_name, p1.contact_email, p1.contact_phone, p1.created_at, p1.deactivated_at, p1.deactivation_reason, p1.description, p1.total_reviews, p1.updated_at, p1.user_id, p1.website_url
FROM (
    SELECT p.id, p.avg_rating, p.cancellation_policy, p.city, p.country, p.created_at, p.current_bookings, p.description, p.destination, p.duration_days, p.duration_nights, p.is_featured, p.max_capacity, p.min_age, p.packager_id, p.status, p.title, p.total_reviews, p.package_type, p.updated_at
    FROM packages AS p
    WHERE p.status = 'published'::package_status AND EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM package_seasonal_pricing AS p0
        WHERE p.id = p0.package_id AND p0.is_active AND p0.end_date >= @__today_0)
    ORDER BY p.created_at DESC
    LIMIT @__p_2 OFFSET @__p_1
) AS t
INNER JOIN packagers AS p1 ON t.packager_id = p1.id
LEFT JOIN package_media AS p2 ON t.id = p2.package_id
LEFT JOIN package_seasonal_pricing AS p3 ON t.id = p3.package_id
ORDER BY t.created_at DESC, t.id, p1.id, p2.id

SELECT t.id, t.avg_rating, t.cancellation_policy, t.city, t.country, t.created_at, t.current_bookings, t.description, t.destination, t.duration_days, t.duration_nights, t.is_featured, t.max_capacity, t.min_age, t.packager_id, t.status, t.title, t.total_reviews, t.package_type, t.updated_at, p1.id, p2.id, p2.caption, p2.category, p2.display_order, p2.file_name, p2.file_path, p2.file_size_bytes, p2.is_primary, p2.mime_type, p2.package_id, p2.uploaded_at, p3.id, p3.available_slots, p3.base_price, p3.child_price, p3.discount_percent, p3.end_date, p3.is_active, p3.package_id, p3.season_name, p3.start_date, p1.approved_at, p1.approved_by, p1.avg_rating, p1.business_license_no, p1.company_name, p1.contact_email, p1.contact_phone, p1.created_at, p1.deactivated_at, p1.deactivation_reason, p1.description, p1.total_reviews, p1.updated_at, p1.user_id, p1.website_url
FROM (
    SELECT p.id, p.avg_rating, p.cancellation_policy, p.city, p.country, p.created_at, p.current_bookings, p.description, p.destination, p.duration_days, p.duration_nights, p.is_featured, p.max_capacity, p.min_age, p.packager_id, p.status, p.title, p.total_reviews, p.package_type, p.updated_at
    FROM packages AS p

        SELECT 1
        FROM package_seasonal_pricing AS p0
        WHERE p.id = p0.package_id AND p0.is_active AND p0.end_date >= @__today_0)
    ORDER BY p.created_at DESC
    LIMIT @__p_2 OFFSET @__p_1
) AS t

ORDER BY t.created_at DESC, t.id, p1.id, p2.id

    SELECT p.id, p.avg_rating, p.cancellation_policy, p.city, p.country, p.created_at, p.current_bookings, p.description, p.destination, p.duration_days, p.duration_nights, p.is_featured, p.max_capacity, p.min_age, p.packager_id, p.status, p.title, p.total_reviews, p.package_type, p.updated_at, p0.id AS id0, p0.approved_at, p0.approved_by, p0.avg_rating AS avg_rating0, p0.business_license_no, p0.company_name, p0.contact_email, p0.contact_phone, p0.created_at AS created_at0, p0.deactivated_at, p0.deactivation_reason, p0.description AS description0, p0.total_reviews AS total_reviews0, p0.updated_at AS updated_at0, p0.user_id, p0.website_url
    FROM packages AS p
    INNER JOIN packagers AS p0 ON p.packager_id = p0.id
    WHERE p.id = @__packageId_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT i.id, i.created_at, i.day_number, i.description, i.location, i.package_id, i.title, i0.id AS id0, i0.activity_title, i0.activity_type, i0.session, i0.description AS description0, i0.duration_minutes, i0.extra_cost, i0.is_optional, i0.itinerary_day_id, i0.location AS location0, i0.sequence_order, i1.id AS id1, i1.description AS description1, i1.is_included, i1.itinerary_day_id AS itinerary_day_id0, i1.meal, i1.venue, p1.id AS id2, p1.amenities, p1.check_in_time, p1.check_out_time, p1.hotel_address, p1.hotel_name, p1.itinerary_day_id AS itinerary_day_id1, p1.notes, p1.room_type, p1.star_rating, p2.id AS id3, p2.distance_km, p2.drop_point, p2.drop_time, p2.itinerary_day_id AS itinerary_day_id2, p2.notes AS notes0, p2.pickup_point, p2.pickup_time, p2.segment_order, p2.mode, p2.vehicle_description
    FROM itinerary_days AS i
    LEFT JOIN itinerary_activities AS i0 ON i.id = i0.itinerary_day_id
    LEFT JOIN itinerary_day_meals AS i1 ON i.id = i1.itinerary_day_id
    LEFT JOIN package_accommodation AS p1 ON i.id = p1.itinerary_day_id
    LEFT JOIN package_transport AS p2 ON i.id = p2.itinerary_day_id
) AS t0 ON t.id = t0.package_id
LEFT JOIN package_highlights AS p3 ON t.id = p3.package_id
LEFT JOIN package_inclusions AS p4 ON t.id = p4.package_id
LEFT JOIN package_media AS p5 ON t.id = p5.package_id
LEFT JOIN package_seasonal_pricing AS p6 ON t.id = p6.package_id
LEFT JOIN reviews AS r ON t.id = r.package_id
ORDER BY t.id, t.id0, t0.id, t0.id0, t0.id1, t0.id2, t0.id3, p3.id, p4.id, p5.id, p6.id

SELECT t.id, t.avg_rating, t.cancellation_policy, t.city, t.country, t.created_at, t.current_bookings, t.description, t.destination, t.duration_days, t.duration_nights, t.is_featured, t.max_capacity, t.min_age, t.packager_id, t.status, t.title, t.total_reviews, t.package_type, t.updated_at, p1.id, p2.id, p2.caption, p2.category, p2.display_order, p2.file_name, p2.file_path, p2.file_size_bytes, p2.is_primary, p2.mime_type, p2.package_id, p2.uploaded_at, p3.id, p3.available_slots, p3.base_price, p3.child_price, p3.discount_percent, p3.end_date, p3.is_active, p3.package_id, p3.season_name, p3.start_date, p1.approved_at, p1.approved_by, p1.avg_rating, p1.business_license_no, p1.company_name, p1.contact_email, p1.contact_phone, p1.created_at, p1.deactivated_at, p1.deactivation_reason, p1.description, p1.total_reviews, p1.updated_at, p1.user_id, p1.website_url
FROM (
    SELECT p.id, p.avg_rating, p.cancellation_policy, p.city, p.country, p.created_at, p.current_bookings, p.description, p.destination, p.duration_days, p.duration_nights, p.is_featured, p.max_capacity, p.min_age, p.packager_id, p.status, p.title, p.total_reviews, p.package_type, p.updated_at
    FROM packages AS p
    WHERE p.status = 'published'::package_status AND EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM package_seasonal_pricing AS p0
        WHERE p.id = p0.package_id AND p0.is_active AND p0.end_date >= @__today_0)
    ORDER BY p.created_at DESC
    LIMIT @__p_2 OFFSET @__p_1
) AS t
INNER JOIN packagers AS p1 ON t.packager_id = p1.id
LEFT JOIN package_media AS p2 ON t.id = p2.package_id
LEFT JOIN package_seasonal_pricing AS p3 ON t.id = p3.package_id
ORDER BY t.created_at DESC, t.id, p1.id, p2.id
